FROM "jobPosts" AS j
INNER JOIN recruiters AS r ON j."RecruiterID" = r.guid
INNER JOIN companies AS c ON r."CompanyId" = c.guid
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT p.guid, p."JobPostId", p."SkillId", s.guid AS guid0, s."Name"
    FROM "postSkills" AS p
    INNER JOIN skills AS s ON p."SkillId" = s.guid
) AS s3 ON j.guid = s3."JobPostId"
LEFT JOIN responsibilities AS r0 ON j.guid = r0."PostId"
LEFT JOIN requirements AS r1 ON j.guid = r1."PostId"
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT j0.guid, j0."AppliedOn", j0."IsDeleted", j0."JobPostId", j0."SeekerId", j0."Status", s0.guid AS guid0, s0."About", s0."ConnectionId", s0."Education", s0."Experience", s0."FirstName", s0."IsDeleted" AS "IsDeleted0", s0."LastName", s0."UserId", s4.guid AS guid1, s4."SeekerId" AS "SeekerId0", s4."SkillId", s4.guid0 AS guid00, s4."Name"
    FROM "jobApplications" AS j0
    INNER JOIN seekers AS s0 ON j0."SeekerId" = s0.guid
    LEFT JOIN (
        SELECT s1.guid, s1."SeekerId", s1."SkillId", s2.guid AS guid0, s2."Name"
        FROM "seekerSkills" AS s1
        INNER JOIN skills AS s2 ON s1."SkillId" = s2.guid
    ) AS s4 ON s0.guid = s4."SeekerId"
) AS s5 ON j.guid = s5."JobPostId"
WHERE NOT (j."IsDeleted")
ORDER BY j.guid, r.guid, c.guid, s3.guid, s3.guid0, r0.guid, r1.guid, s5.guid, s5.guid0, s5.guid1

INNER JOIN recruiters AS r ON j."RecruiterID" = r.guid
INNER JOIN companies AS c ON r."CompanyId" = c.guid
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT p.guid, p."JobPostId", p."SkillId", s.guid AS guid0, s."Name"
    FROM "postSkills" AS p
    INNER JOIN skills AS s ON p."SkillId" = s.guid
) AS s3 ON j.guid = s3."JobPostId"
LEFT JOIN responsibilities AS r0 ON j.guid = r0."PostId"
LEFT JOIN requirements AS r1 ON j.guid = r1."PostId"
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT j0.guid, j0."AppliedOn", j0."IsDeleted", j0."JobPostId", j0."SeekerId", j0."Status", s0.guid AS guid0, s0."About", s0."ConnectionId", s0."Education", s0."Experience", s0."FirstName", s0."IsDeleted" AS "IsDeleted0", s0."LastName", s0."UserId", s4.guid AS guid1, s4."SeekerId" AS "SeekerId0", s4."SkillId", s4.guid0 AS guid00, s4."Name"
    FROM "jobApplications" AS j0
    INNER JOIN seekers AS s0 ON j0."SeekerId" = s0.guid
    LEFT JOIN (
        SELECT s1.guid, s1."SeekerId", s1."SkillId", s2.guid AS guid0, s2."Name"
        FROM "seekerSkills" AS s1
        INNER JOIN skills AS s2 ON s1."SkillId" = s2.guid
    ) AS s4 ON s0.guid = s4."SeekerId"
) AS s5 ON j.guid = s5."JobPostId"
WHERE NOT (j."IsDeleted")
ORDER BY j.guid, r.guid, c.guid, s3.guid, s3.guid0, r0.guid, r1.guid, s5.guid, s5.guid0, s5.guid1

FROM "jobPosts" AS j
INNER JOIN recruiters AS r ON j."RecruiterID" = r.guid
INNER JOIN companies AS c ON r."CompanyId" = c.guid
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT p.guid, p."JobPostId", p."SkillId", s.guid AS guid0, s."Name"
    FROM "postSkills" AS p
    INNER JOIN skills AS s ON p."SkillId" = s.guid
) AS s3 ON j.guid = s3."JobPostId"
LEFT JOIN responsibilities AS r0 ON j.guid = r0."PostId"
LEFT JOIN requirements AS r1 ON j.guid = r1."PostId"
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT j0.guid, j0."AppliedOn", j0."IsDeleted", j0."JobPostId", j0."SeekerId", j0."Status", s0.guid AS guid0, s0."About", s0."ConnectionId", s0."Education", s0."Experience", s0."FirstName", s0."IsDeleted" AS "IsDeleted0", s0."LastName", s0."UserId", s4.guid AS guid1, s4."SeekerId" AS "SeekerId0", s4."SkillId", s4.guid0 AS guid00, s4."Name"
    FROM "jobApplications" AS j0
    INNER JOIN seekers AS s0 ON j0."SeekerId" = s0.guid
    LEFT JOIN (
        SELECT s1.guid, s1."SeekerId", s1."SkillId", s2.guid AS guid0, s2."Name"
        FROM "seekerSkills" AS s1
        INNER JOIN skills AS s2 ON s1."SkillId" = s2.guid
    ) AS s4 ON s0.guid = s4."SeekerId"
) AS s5 ON j.guid = s5."JobPostId"
WHERE NOT (j."IsDeleted")

FROM "jobPosts" AS j
INNER JOIN recruiters AS r ON j."RecruiterID" = r.guid
INNER JOIN companies AS c ON r."CompanyId" = c.guid
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT p.guid, p."JobPostId", p."SkillId", s.guid AS guid0, s."Name"
    FROM "postSkills" AS p
    INNER JOIN skills AS s ON p."SkillId" = s.guid
) AS s3 ON j.guid = s3."JobPostId"
LEFT JOIN responsibilities AS r0 ON j.guid = r0."PostId"
LEFT JOIN requirements AS r1 ON j.guid = r1."PostId"
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT j0.guid, j0."AppliedOn", j0."IsDeleted", j0."JobPostId", j0."SeekerId", j0."Status", s0.guid AS guid0, s0."About", s0."ConnectionId", s0."Education", s0."Experience", s0."FirstName", s0."IsDeleted" AS "IsDeleted0", s0."LastName", s0."UserId", s4.guid AS guid1, s4."SeekerId" AS "SeekerId0", s4."SkillId", s4.guid0 AS guid00, s4."Name"
    FROM "jobApplications" AS j0
    INNER JOIN seekers AS s0 ON j0."SeekerId" = s0.guid
    LEFT JOIN (
        SELECT s1.guid, s1."SeekerId", s1."SkillId", s2.guid AS guid0, s2."Name"
        FROM "seekerSkills" AS s1
        INNER JOIN skills AS s2 ON s1."SkillId" = s2.guid
    ) AS s4 ON s0.guid = s4."SeekerId"
) AS s5 ON j.guid = s5."JobPostId"
WHERE NOT (j."IsDeleted")
ORDER BY j.guid, r.guid, c.guid, s3.guid, s3.guid0, r0.guid, r1.guid, s5.guid, s5.guid0, s5.guid1

        FROM "seekerSkills" AS s1
        INNER JOIN skills AS s2 ON s1."SkillId" = s2.guid
    ) AS s5 ON s0.guid = s5."SeekerId"
) AS s6 ON s3.guid = s6."JobPostId"
ORDER BY s3.guid, s3.guid0, s3.guid1, s4.guid, s4.guid0, r0.guid, r1.guid, s6.guid, s6.guid0, s6.guid1

UPDATE "jobPosts" SET "IsDeleted" = @p0
WHERE guid = @p1;
